### [235] [FIGROTD: A Friendly-to-Handle Dataset for Image Guided Retrieval with Optional Text](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22247)
*Hoang-Bao Le,Allie Tran,Binh T. Nguyen,Liting Zhou,Cathal Gurrin*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: IGROT统一了视觉检索和组合检索，但缺乏可访问的基准和平衡性能的方法。本文提出轻量级数据集FIGROTD和方差引导特征掩码VaGFeM方法，在多个基准上取得竞争性结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 图像引导检索（IGROT）统一了视觉检索（无文本）和组合检索（有文本），在Google Image和Bing等应用中很重要，但进展受到缺乏可访问基准和平衡性能方法的限制。大规模数据集计算成本高，现有模型往往偏向视觉或组合查询。

Method: 1) 引入FIGROTD轻量级高质量数据集，包含16,474个训练三元组和1,262个测试三元组，涵盖CIR、SBIR和CSTBIR任务；2) 提出方差引导特征掩码(VaGFeM)，基于方差统计选择性增强判别性维度；3) 采用双损失设计（InfoNCE + Triplet）改进组合推理。

Result: 在FIGROTD上训练的VaGFeM在九个基准上取得竞争性结果：在CIRCO上达到34.8 mAP@10，在Sketchy上达到75.7 mAP@200，尽管使用较少三元组仍优于更强的基线模型。

Conclusion: 本文提出的FIGROTD数据集和VaGFeM方法有效解决了IGROT领域的基准和方法问题，通过轻量级数据集和选择性特征增强实现了平衡的性能表现，为图像引导检索提供了实用的解决方案。

Abstract: Image-Guided Retrieval with Optional Text (IGROT) unifies visual retrieval (without text) and composed retrieval (with text). Despite its relevance in applications like Google Image and Bing, progress has been limited by the lack of an accessible benchmark and methods that balance performance across subtasks. Large-scale datasets such as MagicLens are comprehensive but computationally prohibitive, while existing models often favor either visual or compositional queries. We introduce FIGROTD, a lightweight yet high-quality IGROT dataset with 16,474 training triplets and 1,262 test triplets across CIR, SBIR, and CSTBIR. To reduce redundancy, we propose the Variance Guided Feature Mask (VaGFeM), which selectively enhances discriminative dimensions based on variance statistics. We further adopt a dual-loss design (InfoNCE + Triplet) to improve compositional reasoning. Trained on FIGROTD, VaGFeM achieves competitive results on nine benchmarks, reaching 34.8 mAP@10 on CIRCO and 75.7 mAP@200 on Sketchy, outperforming stronger baselines despite fewer triplets.

</details>


### [236] [UNION: A Lightweight Target Representation for Efficient Zero-Shot Image-Guided Retrieval with Optional Textual Queries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22253)
*Hoang-Bao Le,Allie Tran,Binh T. Nguyen,Liting Zhou,Cathal Gurrin*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: UNION方法通过融合图像嵌入和空文本提示，在少量数据监督下解决图像引导检索问题，在CIR和SBIR任务上取得竞争性结果


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决图像引导检索（IGROT）在低数据监督下的挑战，统一组合图像检索（CIR）和基于草图的图像检索（SBIR）两个主要任务

Method: 提出UNION方法，轻量级且可泛化的目标表示，将图像嵌入与空文本提示融合，无需修改预训练视觉语言模型架构

Result: 仅用5,000个训练样本，在CIRCO基准上达到mAP@50为38.5，在Sketchy基准上达到mAP@200为82.7，超越许多强监督基线

Conclusion: UNION方法展示了在少量数据下跨不同查询类型桥接视觉和语言的鲁棒性和效率

Abstract: Image-Guided Retrieval with Optional Text (IGROT) is a general retrieval setting where a query consists of an anchor image, with or without accompanying text, aiming to retrieve semantically relevant target images. This formulation unifies two major tasks: Composed Image Retrieval (CIR) and Sketch-Based Image Retrieval (SBIR). In this work, we address IGROT under low-data supervision by introducing UNION, a lightweight and generalisable target representation that fuses the image embedding with a null-text prompt. Unlike traditional approaches that rely on fixed target features, UNION enhances semantic alignment with multimodal queries while requiring no architectural modifications to pretrained vision-language models. With only 5,000 training samples - from LlavaSCo for CIR and Training-Sketchy for SBIR - our method achieves competitive results across benchmarks, including CIRCO mAP@50 of 38.5 and Sketchy mAP@200 of 82.7, surpassing many heavily supervised baselines. This demonstrates the robustness and efficiency of UNION in bridging vision and language across diverse query types.

</details>


### [237] [Efficiency and Effectiveness of SPLADE Models on Billion-Scale Web Document Title](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22263)
*Taeryun Won,Tae Kwan Lee,Hiun Kim,Hyemin Lee*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文比较了BM25、SPLADE和Expanded-SPLADE在大规模网页文档检索中的效果与效率，发现SPLADE模型在复杂查询上表现更优但计算成本更高，通过剪枝策略可在保持性能的同时提升效率，其中Expanded-SPLADE在效果与效率间达到最佳平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大规模网页文档检索中，传统BM25模型虽然高效但在复杂查询上表现有限，而基于稀疏词法表示的SPLADE模型虽然性能更优但计算成本较高。需要研究如何在保持检索效果的同时提升这些先进模型的效率，以便在实际搜索引擎中部署。

Method: 1. 在从数千万到数十亿规模的网页文档标题数据集上对比BM25、SPLADE和Expanded-SPLADE模型；2. 引入剪枝策略包括文档中心剪枝、top-k查询词选择、带词项阈值的布尔查询；3. 评估这些策略在降低计算成本的同时对检索性能的影响。

Result: 1. SPLADE和Expanded-SPLADE在检索性能上优于BM25，特别是在复杂查询上；2. 这些模型的计算成本显著高于BM25；3. 提出的剪枝策略有效降低了计算成本，同时保持了大部分检索性能；4. Expanded-SPLADE在效果与效率间达到最佳平衡，尤其适合处理大规模数据集。

Conclusion: 稀疏检索模型如SPLADE和Expanded-SPLADE在大规模网页文档检索中具有性能优势，但需要适当的优化策略来平衡效果与效率。Expanded-SPLADE结合剪枝策略是实际部署的最佳选择，为大规模搜索引擎中稀疏检索模型的部署提供了有价值的指导。

Abstract: This paper presents a comprehensive comparison of BM25, SPLADE, and Expanded-SPLADE models in the context of large-scale web document retrieval. We evaluate the effectiveness and efficiency of these models on datasets spanning from tens of millions to billions of web document titles. SPLADE and Expanded-SPLADE, which utilize sparse lexical representations, demonstrate superior retrieval performance compared to BM25, especially for complex queries. However, these models incur higher computational costs. We introduce pruning strategies, including document-centric pruning and top-k query term selection, boolean query with term threshold to mitigate these costs and improve the models' efficiency without significantly sacrificing retrieval performance. The results show that Expanded-SPLADE strikes the best balance between effectiveness and efficiency, particularly when handling large datasets. Our findings offer valuable insights for deploying sparse retrieval models in large-scale search engines.

</details>


### [238] [FedAU2: Attribute Unlearning for User-Level Federated Recommender Systems with Adaptive and Robust Adversarial Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22872)
*Yuyuan Li,Junjie Fang,Fengyuan Yu,Xichun Sheng,Tianyu Du,Xuyang Teng,Shaowei Jiang,Linbo Jiang,Jianan Lin,Chaochao Chen*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: FedAU2：一种针对用户级联邦推荐系统的属性遗忘方法，通过自适应对抗训练和双随机变分自编码器解决训练不稳定性和梯度信息泄露问题


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦推荐系统虽然保护用户隐私，但用户嵌入中仍包含敏感属性信息，易受属性推断攻击。属性遗忘是缓解此问题的有前景方法，但在用户级联邦推荐系统中面临训练不稳定性和梯度信息泄露两大挑战

Method: 提出FedAU2方法：1）自适应对抗训练策略，根据本地优化行为调整训练动态；2）双随机变分自编码器扰动对抗模型，防止基于梯度的信息泄露

Result: 在三个真实世界数据集上的实验表明，FedAU2在遗忘效果和推荐性能方面均优于现有基线方法

Conclusion: FedAU2有效解决了用户级联邦推荐系统中的属性遗忘问题，在保护用户隐私的同时保持了良好的推荐性能

Abstract: Federated Recommender Systems (FedRecs) leverage federated learning to protect user privacy by retaining data locally. However, user embeddings in FedRecs often encode sensitive attribute information, rendering them vulnerable to attribute inference attacks. Attribute unlearning has emerged as a promising approach to mitigate this issue. In this paper, we focus on user-level FedRecs, which is a more practical yet challenging setting compared to group-level FedRecs. Adversarial training emerges as the most feasible approach within this context. We identify two key challenges in implementing adversarial training-based attribute unlearning for user-level FedRecs: i) mitigating training instability caused by user data heterogeneity, and ii) preventing attribute information leakage through gradients. To address these challenges, we propose FedAU2, an attribute unlearning method for user-level FedRecs. For CH1, we propose an adaptive adversarial training strategy, where the training dynamics are adjusted in response to local optimization behavior. For CH2, we propose a dual-stochastic variational autoencoder to perturb the adversarial model, effectively preventing gradient-based information leakage. Extensive experiments on three real-world datasets demonstrate that our proposed FedAU2 achieves superior performance in unlearning effectiveness and recommendation performance compared to existing baselines.

</details>


### [239] [Do LLM-judges Align with Human Relevance in Cranfield-style Recommender Evaluation?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.23312)
*Gustavo Penha,Aleksandr V. Petrov,Claudia Hauff,Enrico Palumbo,Ali Vardasbi,Edoardo D'Amico,Francesco Fabbri,Alice Wang,Praveen Chandar,Henrik Lindstrom,Hugues Bouchard,Mounia Lalmas*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文研究使用大型语言模型作为自动评估器来解决推荐系统评估中的可扩展性问题，通过实验证明LLM评估器与人类评估结果高度一致，并在工业案例中验证了其实际价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推荐系统评估面临长期挑战：基于历史用户交互和训练测试分割的离线方法由于曝光偏差、流行度偏差、采样评估和MNAR模式等问题，往往产生不稳定和不一致的结果。虽然Cranfield风格的测试集合为文本检索提供了稳健评估，但构建这样的集合成本高昂，限制了可扩展性。

Method: 使用ML-32M-ext Cranfield风格电影推荐集合，首先分析现有评估方法的局限性，然后探索LLM评估器与人工提供相关性标签之间的对齐度和推荐系统排序一致性。研究纳入更丰富的项目元数据和更长的用户历史如何改善对齐度。最后通过播客推荐领域的工业案例研究展示LLM评估器在实际模型选择中的应用价值。

Result: 研究发现：1) 纳入更丰富的项目元数据和更长的用户历史可以改善LLM评估器与人类评估的对齐度；2) LLM评估器与基于人类的排序结果高度一致（Kendall's tau = 0.87）；3) 工业案例研究证实LLM评估器在模型选择中具有实际价值。

Conclusion: LLM评估器是评估推荐系统的可行且可扩展的方法，能够解决传统评估方法中的可扩展性挑战，同时保持与人类评估结果的高度一致性。

Abstract: Evaluating recommender systems remains a long-standing challenge, as offline methods based on historical user interactions and train-test splits often yield unstable and inconsistent results due to exposure bias, popularity bias, sampled evaluations, and missing-not-at-random patterns. In contrast, textual document retrieval benefits from robust, standardized evaluation via Cranfield-style test collections, which combine pooled relevance judgments with controlled setups. While recent work shows that adapting this methodology to recommender systems is feasible, constructing such collections remains costly due to the need for manual relevance judgments, thus limiting scalability. This paper investigates whether Large Language Models (LLMs) can serve as reliable automatic judges to address these scalability challenges. Using the ML-32M-ext Cranfield-style movie recommendation collection, we first examine the limitations of existing evaluation methodologies. Then we explore the alignment and the recommender systems ranking agreement between the LLM-judge and human provided relevance labels. We find that incorporating richer item metadata and longer user histories improves alignment, and that LLM-judge yields high agreement with human-based rankings (Kendall's tau = 0.87). Finally, an industrial case study in the podcast recommendation domain demonstrates the practical value of LLM-judge for model selection. Overall, our results show that LLM-judge is a viable and scalable approach for evaluating recommender systems.

</details>

### [240] [The Rapid Growth of AI Foundation Model Usage in Science](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.21739)
*Ana Trišović,Alex Fogelson,Janakan Sivaloganathan,Neil Thompson*

Main category: cs.DL

TL;DR: 对AI基础模型在科学领域使用的大规模分析显示：采用率呈近指数增长，语言学、计算机科学和工程学使用最多；视觉模型最常用但语言模型份额增长；开源模型占主导；科学家使用的模型规模远小于AI构建者开发的模型，且使用较小模型可能限制了AI科学效益


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 首次对AI基础模型在科学领域的实际使用情况进行大规模分析，而不仅仅是引用或关键词分析，旨在了解AI模型在科学研究中的真实采用情况和影响

Method: 通过大规模分析科学文献中AI基础模型的实际使用情况，研究采用率增长趋势、学科分布、模型类型、开源情况、模型规模差异及其与科学影响力的关系

Result: 1) AI基础模型在科学中的采用率呈近指数增长，语言学、计算机科学和工程学使用最多；2) 视觉模型最常用但语言模型份额增长；3) 开源模型占主导；4) 科学家使用的模型规模远小于AI构建者开发的模型（2024年差距达26倍）；5) 使用较大模型的论文出现在更高影响力期刊并获得更多引用

Conclusion: AI基础模型在科学中的采用快速增长，但科学家使用的模型规模远小于最新AI模型，这可能限制了AI在科学中的全部潜力；使用更大模型与更高科学影响力相关，表明模型规模对AI科学效益的重要性

Abstract: We present the first large-scale analysis of AI foundation model usage in science - not just citations or keywords. We find that adoption has grown rapidly, at nearly-exponential rates, with the highest uptake in Linguistics, Computer Science, and Engineering. Vision models are the most used foundation models in science, although language models' share is growing. Open-weight models dominate. As AI builders increase the parameter counts of their models, scientists have followed suit but at a much slower rate: in 2013, the median foundation model built was 7.7x larger than the median one adopted in science, by 2024 this had jumped to 26x. We also present suggestive evidence that scientists' use of these smaller models may be limiting them from getting the full benefits of AI-enabled science, as papers that use larger models appear in higher-impact journals and accrue more citations.

</details>


### [241] [Who Owns the Knowledge? Copyright, GenAI, and the Future of Academic Publishing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.21755)
*Dmitry Kochetkov*

Main category: cs.DL

TL;DR: 本文探讨生成式AI和大型语言模型在科研与高等教育中的整合，分析其对版权法和开放科学原则的挑战，指出当前监管框架存在重大漏洞，呼吁建立国际协调立法保护知识产权和科学完整性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式AI和大型语言模型在科研与高等教育中的整合带来了革命性机遇，但同时也引发了深刻的伦理、法律和监管问题。当前监管框架在关键司法管辖区存在显著漏洞，特别是在使用受版权保护作品和开放科学成果进行AI训练方面。

Method: 本研究通过分析美国、中国、欧盟和英国等关键司法管辖区的现行监管框架，探讨版权法和开放科学原则面临的挑战。研究评估了广泛采用的许可机制（如Creative Commons）在AI训练方面的不足，并分析AI系统中普遍缺乏署名的问题如何挑战既有的原创性概念。

Result: 研究发现当前监管框架存在重大漏洞，AI训练不应受到合理使用例外的保护。作者应有权拒绝将其作品用于AI训练，大学应在塑造负责任的AI治理中发挥主导作用。广泛采用的许可机制无法充分应对AI训练的复杂性。

Conclusion: 迫切需要国际协调的立法努力，以确保透明度、保护知识产权，并防止出现可能将商业利润置于科学完整性和公平知识生产之上的寡头垄断市场结构。

Abstract: The integration of generative artificial intelligence (GenAI) and large language models (LLMs) into scientific research and higher education presents a paradigm shift, offering revolutionizing opportunities while simultaneously raising profound ethical, legal, and regulatory questions. This study examines the complex intersection of AI and science, with a specific focus on the challenges posed to copyright law and the principles of open science. The author argues that current regulatory frameworks in key jurisdictions like the United States, China, the European Union, and the United Kingdom, while aiming to foster innovation, contain significant gaps, particularly concerning the use of copyrighted works and open science outputs for AI training. Widely adopted licensing mechanisms, such as Creative Commons, fail to adequately address the nuances of AI training, and the pervasive lack of attribution within AI systems fundamentally challenges established notions of originality. This paper issues a call to action, contending that AI training should not be shielded under fair use exceptions. Instead, the author advocates for upholding authors' rights to refuse the use of their works for AI training and proposes that universities assume a leading role in shaping responsible AI governance. The conclusion is that a harmonized international legislative effort is urgently needed to ensure transparency, protect intellectual property, and prevent the emergence of an oligopolistic market structure that could prioritize commercial profit over scientific integrity and equitable knowledge production.

</details>

*Zekai Zhang*

Abstract: This article aims to propose and elucidate the analytical concepts of "individual scientist" and "integrated scientist" to depict the fundamental transformation in the modes of scientific research actors throughout the history of science. The "individual scientist" represents an early modern scientific research panel characterized by independence, egalitarian collaboration, and personal recognition, while the "integrated scientist" emerged in the context of "big science," marked by hierarchical teams, division of labor, collaboration, and the concentration of recognition on team leaders. Through historical review and case analysis, this article explores the underlying drivers of this transformation and focuses on its challenges and reconstructions concerning the name-based scientific reward system, aiming to provide a reflective perspective for contemporary scientific governance and research evaluation.

### [243] [Research on Diamond Open Access in the Long Shadow of Science Policy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22965)

Abstract: This paper reviews research literature on Diamond Open Access (DOA) journals - sometimes also called Platinum Open Access - that was produced after this journal segment started to become a priority in European research policy around 2020. It contextualizes the current science policy debate, critically examines different understandings of DOA, and reviews studies on the role of such journals in scholarly communication. Most existing research consists of quantitative studies focusing on aspects such as the number of DOA journals, their publication output, the diversity of the landscape in terms of subject areas, languages, publishing entities, indexing in major databases, awareness and perception among scholars, cost analyses, as well as insights into the internal operations of DOA journals. The review shows that research on DOA journals is partly influenced by the science policy discourse in at least two ways: first, through the normativity inherent in that discourse, and second, through the temporality of policy-driven research of practical relevance, which leaves important aspects of the phenomenon understudied. Moreover, research on the DOA journal landscape has implications beyond understanding this particular journal segment, as it also challenges established views of the global system of scholarly communication.

### [244] [ML Researchers Support Openness in Peer Review But Are Concerned About Resubmission Bias](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.23439)
*Vishisht Rao,Justin Payan,Andrew McCallum,Nihar B. Shah*

Main category: cs.DL

TL;DR: 该研究调查了机器学习领域2,385名同行评审参与者对开放评审政策的看法，发现大多数人支持发布已接受论文的评审意见，但担心拒稿偏见和评审者去匿名化风险。研究还发现完全开放评审的会议（ICLR）比部分开放评审的会议（NeurIPS）在评审质量上略有优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着同行评审场所越来越多地采用开放评审政策，公开匿名评审意见并允许公众评论，但各场所采用的政策不同，关于开放评审利弊的争论仍在继续。本研究旨在通过调查机器学习领域同行评审参与者的经验和意见，为这一讨论提供实证依据。

Method: 研究采用混合方法：1）对2,385名机器学习领域的评审者、作者和其他同行评审参与者进行问卷调查；2）使用AI标注了4,244篇来自ICLR（完全开放）和NeurIPS（部分开放）的评审意见，比较两个会议在正确性、完整性和论证充分性方面的差异。

Result: 主要发现：1）超过80%受访者支持发布已接受论文的评审意见，但只有27.1%支持发布被拒稿件；2）主要益处包括提高公众理解、评审者教育、增加公平性和激励高质量评审；3）主要挑战是拒稿偏见（41%受访者认为影响最大）和评审者去匿名化风险；4）完全开放的ICLR在正确性和完整性方面略优于部分开放的NeurIPS，但效应值较小且统计显著；5）在论证充分性方面无显著差异。

Conclusion: 开放评审政策在机器学习社区获得广泛支持，特别是对于已接受论文的评审公开。然而，拒稿偏见是主要担忧。完全开放评审可能带来轻微的质量提升，但需要平衡透明度和评审者保护。研究为开放评审政策的制定提供了实证依据，并发布了完整数据集供进一步研究。

Abstract: Peer-review venues have increasingly adopted open reviewing policies that publicly release anonymized reviews and permit public commenting. Venues have adopted a variety of policies, and there is still ongoing debate about the benefits and drawbacks of decisions. To inform this debate, we surveyed 2,385 reviewers, authors, and other peer-review participants in machine learning to understand their experiences and opinions. Our key findings are:
  (a) Preferences: Over 80% of respondents support releasing reviews for accepted papers and allowing public comments. However, only 27.1% support releasing rejected manuscripts.
  (b) Benefits: Respondents cite improved public understanding (75.3%) and reviewer education (57.8%), increased fairness (56.6%), and stronger incentives for high-quality reviews (48.0%).
  (c) Challenges: The top concern is resubmission bias, where rejection history biases future reviewers (ranked top impact of open reviewing by 41% of respondents, and mentioned in over 50% of free responses). Other challenges include fear of reviewer de-anonymization (33.2%) and potential commenting abuse.
  (d) AI and open peer review: Participants believe open policies deter "AI slop" submissions (71.9%) and AI-generated reviews (38.9%). Respondents are split regarding peer-review venues generating official AI reviews, with 56.0% opposed and 44.0% supportive.
  Finally, we use AI to annotate 4,244 reviews from ICLR (fully open) and NeurIPS (partially open). We find that the fully open venue (ICLR) has higher levels of correctness and completeness than the partially open venue (NeurIPS). The effect size is small for correctness and very small for completeness, and both are statistically significant. We also find that there is no statistically significant difference in the level of substantiation. We release the full dataset at https://github.com/justinpayan/OpenReviewAnalysis.

</details>

### [245] [Automated Enumeration of Reconfigurable Architectures for Thermal Management Systems in Battery Electric Vehicles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.21855)
*Reihaneh Jahedan,Satya Peddada,Mark Jennings,Sunil Katragadda,James Allison,Nenad Miljkovic*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于图建模的系统化方法，用于自动枚举和模拟可重构热管理系统架构，并通过多目标优化在性能、能耗和复杂度之间进行权衡研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着汽车电气化发展，纯电动汽车热管理系统的设计变得复杂，电池性能对温度敏感、缺乏废热、热管理系统能耗对续航里程影响显著。现有研究主要关注特定环境条件下的系统优化，缺乏对可重构架构全面潜力的系统性研究，依赖专家直觉限制了性能提升。

Method: 采用图建模方法对热管理系统架构进行建模，提出系统化方法自动枚举和模拟可重构架构，建立框架进行瞬态性能分析和基于优化的权衡研究，自动创建MATLAB Simscape模型进行评估。

Result: 探索了150多种运行模式序列，保留了39个独特架构进行进一步评估，通过多目标优化结果为基于用户优先级的架构选择提供决策支持。

Conclusion: 提出的系统化方法能够有效探索可重构热管理系统架构的设计空间，通过自动枚举和模拟克服了依赖专家直觉的限制，为纯电动汽车热管理系统设计提供了基于优化的决策支持框架。

Abstract: As the automotive industry moves towards vehicle electrification, designing and optimizing thermal management systems (TMSs) for Battery Electric Vehicles (BEVs) has become a critical focus in recent years. The dependence of battery performance on operating temperature, the lack of waste combustion heat, and the significant effect of TMS energy consumption on driving range make the design of BEV TMSs highly complicated compared to conventional vehicles. Although prior research has focused on optimizing the configuration of thermal systems for varying ambient conditions, a holistic approach to studying the full potential of reconfigurable TMS architectures has not yet been fully explored. The complex design landscape of multi-mode reconfigurable systems is difficult to navigate. Relying solely on expert intuition and creativity to identify new architectures both restricts progress and leaves significant performance improvements unrealized. In this study, using graph modelling of TMS architectures, we propose a systematic method to automatically enumerate and simulate reconfigurable architectures for a TMS, given the desired operating modes, along with a framework to conduct transient performance analysis and optimization-based trade-off studies among system performance, energy consumption, and complexity. We explored more than 150 operating mode sequences, retaining 39 unique architectures for further evaluation. MATLAB Simscape models of these architectures were automatically created and their performance evaluated. The multi-objective optimization results provide decision support for selecting the best architecture based on user priorities.

</details>


### [246] [Quantized Distributed Estimation with Event-triggered Communication and Packet Loss](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.21906)
*Ying Wang,Yanlong Zhao,Ji-Feng Zhang,Karl Henrik Johansson*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合事件触发通信、量化通信和量化测量的分布式估计算法，通过引入一比特信息重构方法处理丢包问题，实现了通信比特率的降低和算法的收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在分布式估计中，减少传输比特数是一个重要目标。事件触发通信和量化通信可以有效降低通信开销，但面临无法区分未触发事件和丢包事件的挑战，这阻碍了算法的有效实现。

Method: 提出事件触发的分布式估计算法，结合量化通信和量化测量。引入一比特信息重构方法来处理丢包问题，确保在通信不可靠情况下仍能进行有效估计。

Result: 建立了算法的几乎必然收敛性和收敛速率，证明了全局平均通信比特率随时间趋于零。揭示了通信速率与收敛速率之间的权衡关系，为设计满足特定收敛速率的通信速率提供了指导。

Conclusion: 所提出的算法在减少通信开销的同时保证了估计性能，通过数值示例验证了理论结果的有效性，为分布式系统中的资源受限通信提供了实用解决方案。

Abstract: This paper focuses on the problem of quantized distributed estimation with event-triggered communication and packet loss, aiming to reduce the number of transmitted bits. The main challenge lies in the inability to differentiate between an untriggered event and a packet loss occurrence. This paper proposes an event-triggered distributed estimation algorithm with quantized communication and quantized measurement, in which it introduces a one-bit information reconstruction method to deal with packet loss. The almost sure convergence and convergence rate of the proposed algorithm are established.Besides, it is demonstrated that the global average communication bit-rate decreases to zero over time. Moreover, the trade-off between communication rate and convergence rate is revealed, providing guidance for designing the communication rate required to achieve the algorithm's convergence rate. A numerical example is supplied to validate the findings.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在基准研究中，当真实系统动态未知或不可用时，传统的协方差估计无法反映实际估计误差，需要蒙特卡洛模拟计算量大，需要更高效的性能预测方法

Method: 推导了具有线性时间复杂度的递归均方误差表达式，考虑了测量模型不匹配，为固定状态轨迹提供准确性能预测

Abstract: We propose analytical mean square error (MSE) expressions for the Kalman filter (KF) and the Kalman smoother (KS) for benchmark studies, where the true system dynamics are unknown or unavailable to the estimator. In such cases, as in benchmark evaluations for target tracking, the analysis relies on deterministic state trajectories. This setting introduces a model mismatch between the estimator and the system, causing the covariance estimates to no longer reflect the actual estimation errors. To enable accurate performance prediction for fixed state trajectories without relying on computationally intensive Monte Carlo simulations, we derive recursive MSE expressions with linear time complexity. The proposed framework also accounts for measurement model mismatch and provides an efficient tool for performance evaluation in benchmark studies with long trajectories. Simulation results confirm the accuracy and computational efficiency of the proposed method.

### [248] [CBF Based Quadratic Program for Trajectory Tracking of Underatuated Marine Vessels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22091)
*Ji-Hong Li*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 船舶的二输入三输出二阶跟踪模型通过极坐标变换可简化为二输入二输出反馈形式，但变换后的系统不符合严格反馈结构，在递归控制器设计中设计虚拟输入的稳定函数时可能出现奇异性。此外，极坐标变换本身也会引入奇异性。

Method: 采用控制障碍函数(CBF)方法，将轨迹跟踪问题表述为二次规划(QP)问题，通过QP优化器求解。

Result: 通过数值仿真验证了所提方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 提出的CBF和QP方法能够有效解决船舶轨迹跟踪中的奇异性问题，为船舶控制系统设计提供了新思路。

Abstract: By introducing two polar coordinates transformations, the marine vessel's original two-input-three-output second-order tracking model can be reduced to a two-input-two-output feedback form. However, the resulting system does not confirm to the strict-feedback structure, leading to potential singularity when designing the stabilizing function for the virtual input in the recursive controller design. Moreover, the polar coordinate transformation itself inherently introduces singularities. To address these singularity issues, this paper employs a control barrier function (CBF) based approach and formulates the trajectory tracking problem as a quadratic program (QP) solved via a QP optimizer. Numerical simulations are carried out to demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed method.

</details>


### [249] [Output-Feedback Stabilizing Policy Iteration for Convergence Assurance of Unknown Discrete-Time Systems with Unmeasurable States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22160)
*Dongdong Li,Jiuxiang Dong*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 提出一种基于数据驱动的输出反馈稳定策略迭代方法，用于状态不可测的未知线性离散时间系统，解决了传统方法需要初始稳定控制策略的难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有策略迭代方法需要从稳定控制策略开始，这对于未知系统（特别是状态不可测的情况）尤其困难，难以保证稳定性和收敛性能。

Method: 引入累积标量参数将原系统压缩到稳定尺度，然后通过整合改进的策略迭代与参数更新规则，逐步放大/恢复到原系统同时保持稳定性，整个过程仅依赖输入输出数据。

Result: 开发了输出反馈稳定策略迭代框架，能够学习闭环稳定控制策略并确保收敛性能，提供了输出反馈的稳定性分析，并通过仿真验证了所提方法。

Conclusion: 该方法成功解决了未知线性离散时间系统在状态不可测情况下的稳定控制策略学习问题，仅使用输入输出数据即可实现闭环稳定控制。

Abstract: This note proposes a data-driven output-feedback stabilizing policy iteration for unknown linear discrete-time systems with unmeasurable states. Existing policy iteration methods for optimal control must start from a stabilizing control policy, which is particularly challenging to obtain for unknown systems, especially when states are unavailable. In such cases, it is more difficult to guarantee stability and convergence performance. To address this problem, an output-feedback stabilizing policy iteration framework is developed to learn closed-loop stabilizing control policies while ensuring convergence performance. Specifically, cumulative scalar parameters are introduced to compress the original system to a stable scale. Then, by integrating modified policy iteration with parameter update rules, the system is gradually amplified/restored to the original system while preserving stability such that the stabilizing control policy is obtained. The entire process is driven solely by input-output data. Moreover, a stability analysis is provided for output-feedback. The proposed approach is validated by simulations.

### [250] [An Equality Set Projection Approach for TSO-DSO Coordination Dispatch](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22179)
*Bo Li,Xicong Pang,Guangrui Wei,Haiwang Zhong,Grant Ruan,Zhengmao Li,Edris Pouresmaeil*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于加速非迭代等式集投影算法的TSO-DSO协调优化调度方法，解决了传统迭代方法收敛效率低和非迭代方法处理高维可行域困难的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着高渗透率分布式能源接入，输配电系统协调优化调度对系统安全和效率至关重要。现有方法中，迭代方法计算收敛效率低，而非迭代方法难以处理高维可行域投影问题。

Method: 采用加速非迭代等式集投影算法：1) 使用ESP算法克服高维可行域构建瓶颈；2) 提出基于正则化的加速方法，降低退化情况下的计算负担；3) 通过相邻面搜索构建可行域投影。

Result: 在多面体数据集、IEEE 33节点系统和T118D10 TSO-DSO系统上的案例研究表明，所提出的协调调度方法具有有效性和计算高效性。

Conclusion: 提出的加速ESP算法能够有效构建高维可行域投影，对顶点数量增加不敏感，显著提升了TSO-DSO协调优化调度的计算效率。

Abstract: Coordinated optimization dispatch (COD) of transmission system operator (TSO) and distribution system operator (DSO) can effectively ensure system security and efficiency under high-penetration distributed energy resource (DER) integration. Researches of large-scale COD problem can be categorized into iterative approaches that allow DSO to dispatch independently, and non-iterative methods based on projections of feasible regions (FR). However, the iterative methods suffer from low computational convergence and efficiency, while non-iterative methods struggle to solve equivalent projections with high-dimensional FR. To address these issues, this paper proposes a TSO-DSO coordinated dispatch approach based on an accelerated non-iterative Equality Set Projection (ESP) algorithm. First, ESP algorithm is employed to overcome the bottleneck of high-dimensional FR construction. Second, an regularization-based accelerated method is proposed to reduce computational burden when degeneracy occurs. Accelerated ESP algorithm constructs projection of FR via adjacent facet searching. Therefore, it is less sensitive to the increase of vertices and could efficiently construct the projection of high-dimensional FR. Case studies on a polyhedron dataset, IEEE 33-Bus System and T118D10 TSO-DSO system demonstrate the effectiveness and computational efficiency of the proposed COD approach.

</details>


### [251] [Joint Scheduling of Workload Demand and Energy Supply in Low-carbon Data Centers with Decision-Dependent Uncertainty Set](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22244)
*Maoyuan Ma,Wangyi Guo,Lei Yang,Zhanbo Xu,Xiaohong Guan*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低碳互联网数据中心中随机工作负载的时空转移特性与氢能分布式能源系统的联合调度面临挑战：工作负载难以准确预测导致系统效率下降和运营成本增加，且工作负载调度决策会影响其随机性，使问题更加复杂。

Method: 1. 提出基于决策依赖不确定性集的工作负载分类模型，明确识别不同类型随机工作负载的时空弹性，并将决策依赖关系描述为线性约束；2. 建立混合整数规划模型优化工作负载需求和能源供应的调度；3. 开发滚动时域算法确保非预期性和全场景可行性，增强系统对高波动性场景的韧性。

Result: 数值测试表明，与基准方法相比，所提方法在大多数不确定场景下能做出有效的工作负载调度决策，并显著降低能源运营成本。

Abstract: This paper addresses the joint scheduling problem of stochastic workloads and a hydrogen-enabled distributed energy system in a low-carbon Internet data centers (IDC). Although such workloads can be shifted over temporal and spatial horizons, it poses challenges when they cannot be accurately predicted, resulting in significant efficiency degradation and high operational cost of the energy system. The problem becomes even more difficult when the workload shifting decisions would influence their randomness, which is natural for the IDC workloads. To tackle these issues, we propose a workload classification model based on the decision-dependent uncertainty set, where the spatiotemporal elasticity of different types of random workloads are clearly identified and the decision dependencies are explicitly described as linear constraints. Thus, a mixed integer program is then established for the optimal scheduling of both workload demand and energy supply. To enhance system resilience against high volatility scenarios, a rolling horizon algorithm is developed to ensure nonanticipativity and full-scenario feasibility. Numerical tests demonstrate that the proposed method exhibits effective workload scheduling decisions with dramatic energy operational cost reductions compared to the benchmarks under most of the uncertain scenarios.

### [252] [Learning the MPC objective function from human preferences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22502)
*Pablo Krupa,Hasna El Hasnaouy,Mario Zanon,Alberto Bemporad*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 该论文提出使用基于偏好的学习方法，从人类对轨迹对的偏好中学习MPC目标函数，通过机器学习分类任务构建替代模型，并将其直接用作MPC目标函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在模型预测控制中，目标函数的设计对闭环系统行为至关重要，但在实际应用中，设计目标函数面临挑战，需要平衡复杂的权衡关系，并准确捕捉难以用量化目标函数表达的性能标准。

Method: 采用基于偏好的学习方法，将学习问题构建为机器学习分类任务，学习一个替代模型来估计一条轨迹优于另一条轨迹的可能性，该替代模型可直接用作MPC目标函数。

Result: 数值结果表明，该方法能够学习到与表达的人类偏好一致的客观函数，从而产生符合人类偏好的闭环轨迹。

Abstract: In Model Predictive Control (MPC), the objective function plays a central role in determining the closed-loop behavior of the system, and must therefore be designed to achieve the desired closed-loop performance. However, in real-world scenarios, its design is often challenging, as it requires balancing complex trade-offs and accurately capturing a performance criterion that may not be easily quantifiable in terms of an objective function. This paper explores preference-based learning as a data-driven approach to constructing an objective function from human preferences over trajectory pairs. We formulate the learning problem as a machine learning classification task to learn a surrogate model that estimates the likelihood of a trajectory being preferred over another. The approach provides a surrogate model that can directly be used as an MPC objective function. Numerical results show that we can learn objective functions that provide closed-loop trajectories that align with the expressed human preferences.

### [253] [Optimal Singular Perturbation-based Model Reduction for Heterogeneous Power Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22728)
*Yue Huang,Dixant B. Sapkota,Manish K. Singh*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文提出了两种基于奇异摄动的方法，用于在缺乏状态物理意义先验知识的情况下，最优识别电力系统中应简化的快速状态，以应对现代电力系统模型异质性和黑盒特性的挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代电力系统因非常规发电和消费技术的出现而规模急剧增长、复杂性增加。传统基于奇异摄动的模型降维方法依赖于对系统状态物理意义的先验知识，但现代电力系统组件模型具有异质性和黑盒特性，挑战了传统方法的技术假设。

Method: 提出了两种奇异摄动方法：1）基于贪心优化的方法，顺序选择要简化的状态；2）基于非线性优化的方法，允许状态变换同时获得最优简化模型。两种方法都采用时间尺度无关的奇异摄动公式，无需系统状态的物理意义先验知识。

Result: 在包含同步电机、逆变器和线路动态的测试系统上进行数值研究，证明了所提方法具有通用性和准确性。

Conclusion: 所提出的奇异摄动方法能够有效处理现代电力系统模型的异质性和黑盒特性，无需状态物理意义的先验知识即可实现模型降维，为复杂电力系统动态分析提供了新的工具。

Abstract: Power systems are globally experiencing an unprecedented growth in size and complexity due to the advent of nonconventional generation and consumption technologies. To navigate computational complexity, power system dynamic models are often reduced using techniques based on singular perturbation. However, several technical assumptions enabling traditional approaches are being challenged due to the heterogeneous, and often black-box, nature of modern power system component models. This work proposes two singular perturbation approaches that aim to optimally identify fast states that shall be reduced, without prior knowledge about the physical meaning of system states. After presenting a timescale-agnostic formulation for singular perturbation, the first approach uses greedy optimization to sequentially select states to be reduced. The second approach relies on a nonlinear optimization routine allowing state transformations while obtaining an optimally reduced model. Numerical studies on a test system featuring synchronous machines, inverters, and line dynamics demonstrate the generalizability and accuracy of the developed approaches.

</details>


### [254] [Switching-time bioprocess control with pulse-width-modulated optogenetics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22893)
*Sebastián Espinel-Ríos*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文提出使用强化学习优化脉冲宽度调制光遗传学控制，通过占空比参数化控制动作，解决传统强度控制中剂量响应关系陡峭时难以精细调控的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光遗传学通过光调控基因表达，可用于动态代谢控制和细胞生长调控。然而，当剂量响应关系（光强度与基因表达强度关系）陡峭时，仅依赖强度控制难以实现中间水平的精细调控，只能实现完全激活或完全抑制。脉冲宽度调制可以缓解这一问题，但优化这种控制需要解决多周期二进制输入的切换时间最优控制问题，传统混合整数规划方法随着时间网格分辨率和周期数增加会变得难以处理。

Method: 提出基于强化学习的替代方案。通过占空比参数化控制动作，占空比是一个连续变量，编码每个强制周期内ON到OFF的切换时间，从而尊重光强度的内在二进制特性。这种方法避免了传统混合整数规划方法中决策变量随时间和周期数快速增长的问题。

Result: 该方法理论上能够有效解决脉冲宽度调制光遗传学控制中的优化问题，通过连续变量参数化二进制控制动作，提高了控制问题的可处理性和优化效率。

Conclusion: 强化学习方法为脉冲宽度调制光遗传学控制提供了一种有效的优化框架，通过占空比参数化控制动作，既尊重了光强度的二进制特性，又避免了传统混合整数规划方法的可扩展性问题，有望实现更精细的生物过程调控。

Abstract: Biotechnology can benefit from dynamic control to improve production efficiency. In this context, optogenetics enables modulation of gene expression using light as an external input, allowing fine-tuning of protein levels to unlock dynamic metabolic control and regulation of cell growth. Optogenetic systems can be actuated by light intensity. However, relying solely on intensity-driven control (i.e., signal amplitude) may fail to properly tune optogenetic bioprocesses when the dose-response relationship (i.e., light intensity versus gene-expression strength) is steep. In these cases, tunability is effectively constrained to either fully active or fully repressed gene expression, with little intermediate regulation. Pulse-width modulation, a concept widely used in electronics, can alleviate this issue by alternating between fully ON and OFF light intensity within forcing periods, thereby smoothing the average response and enhancing process controllability. Naturally, optimizing pulse-width-modulated optogenetics entails a switching-time optimal control problem with a binary input over many forcing periods. While this can be formulated as a mixed-integer program on a refined time grid, the number of decision variables can grow rapidly with increasing time-grid resolution and number of forcing periods, compromising tractability. Here, we propose an alternative solution based on reinforcement learning. We parametrize control actions via the duty cycle, a continuous variable that encodes the ON-to-OFF switching time within each forcing period, thereby respecting the intrinsic binary nature of the light intensity.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据驱动预测控制(DeePC)面临两个基本挑战：计算复杂度随数据集大小呈立方增长，以及数据损坏导致的严重性能下降

Method: 通过影响函数分析推导敏感性评分，量化每个轨迹段对优化解的影响，选择低敏感性段；针对非线性系统，采用两阶段在线选择方法，并用LiSSA算法加速

Result: RDS-DeePC实现了计算效率提升和自动异常值过滤，无需数据质量标签

Abstract: Data-Enabled Predictive Control (DeePC) offers a powerful model-free approach to predictive control, but faces two fundamental challenges: computational complexity scaling cubically with dataset size, and severe performance degradation from corrupted data. This paper introduces Robust Data Selection DeePC (RDS-DeePC), which addresses both challenges through influence function analysis. We derive a sensitivity score quantifying each trajectory segment's leverage on the optimization solution, proving that high-sensitivity segments correspond to outliers while low-sensitivity segments represent consistent data. By selecting low-sensitivity segments, RDS-DeePC achieves computational efficiency and automatic outlier filtering without requiring data quality labels. For nonlinear systems, we extend the framework through a two-stage online selection approach accelerated by the LiSSA algorithm.

Method: 首先提出强非线性可检测性概念，作为未知输入状态估计器存在的充要条件；然后基于此概念设计基于移动水平估计的UISE，使用全阶模型和过去/当前测量；进一步收紧可检测性概念，设计更高效的两阶段MHE-based UISE。

Result: 提出的强非线性可检测性概念为UISE存在提供了理论保证；设计的MHE-based UISE能够从噪声采样测量中重构状态，即使对于无界未知输入也能产生有界估计误差；两阶段MHE-based UISE比全阶模型方法计算效率更高。

Conclusion: 本文为非线性系统在未知输入下的状态估计提供了新的理论框架和实用估计器设计，通过植物生长过程的仿真验证了所提方法相对于传统MHE的优越性。

Abstract: This paper considers state estimation for general nonlinear discrete-time systems subject to measurement noise and possibly unbounded unknown inputs. To approach this problem, we first propose the concept of strong nonlinear detectability. This condition is sufficient and necessary for the existence of unknown input state estimators (UISEs), which reconstruct states from noisy sampled measurements and yield bounded estimation error even for unbounded unknown inputs. Based on the proposed detectability notion, a UISE is designed via a moving horizon estimation strategy using a full-order model as well as past and current measurements. Next, we tighten this detectability notion to design a two-stage MHE-based UISE, which is computationally more efficient than the MHE-based UISE using full-order models. In a simulation example with a plant growth process, both variants of MHE-based UISEs are compared with a conventional MHE to illustrate the merits of the developed methods.

</details>


### [265] [A Lyapunov-Based Small-Gain Theorem for Fixed-Time Stability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.23474)
*Michael Tang,Miroslav Krstic,Jorge Poveda*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Lyapunov的小增益方法，用于建立互联动力系统的固定时间稳定性保证。该方法通过子系统固定时间输入到状态稳定性Lyapunov函数和非线性小增益条件，证明整个互联系统的固定时间稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有小增益定理主要针对渐近稳定性和有限时间稳定性，缺乏针对固定时间稳定性的分析工具。本文旨在填补这一空白，为互联动力系统的固定时间稳定性分析提供理论框架。

Method: 提出基于Lyapunov的小增益方法：1）每个子系统具有固定时间输入到状态稳定性Lyapunov函数；2）满足非线性小增益条件；3）通过理论证明整个互联系统的固定时间稳定性。

Result: 证明了当子系统具有固定时间输入到状态稳定性Lyapunov函数且满足非线性小增益条件时，整个互联系统具有固定时间稳定性。该方法填补了现有小增益定理在固定时间稳定性分析方面的空白。

Conclusion: 本文提出的Lyapunov小增益方法为互联动力系统的固定时间稳定性分析提供了有效的理论工具，并通过分析和数值示例验证了方法的有效性，包括在无时间尺度分离的固定时间反馈优化中的应用。

Abstract: This paper introduces a novel Lyapunov-based small-gain methodology for establishing fixed-time stability (FxTS) guarantees in interconnected dynamical systems. Specifically, we consider interconnections in which each subsystem admits an individual fixed-time input-to-state stability (ISS) Lyapunov function that certifies FxT-ISS. We then show that if a nonlinear small-gain condition is satisfied, then the entire interconnected system is FxTS. Our results are analogous to existing Lyapunov-based small-gain theorems developed for asymptotic and finite-time stability, thereby filling an important gap in the stability analysis of interconnected dynamical systems. The proposed theoretical tools are further illustrated through analytical and numerical examples, including an application to fixed-time feedback optimization of dynamical systems without time-scale separation between the plant and the controller.

</details>
